< Review>
This was the most upsetting experience I have ever had taking my child to the dentist. There were an enormous amount of clues I should have picked up on before I let her give him fillings, from billing to various other issues, but nothing was more upsetting than her. Number one she told me when we went in to see her that he had a large amount of cavities. I have now taken those x-rays to a separate dentist to have them evaluated and according to her she didn't see any, however initially I trusted her. She suggested that we don't do them all at once and break it up in 2 appointments. She then asked me if he was afraid of needles.. I said no more that the average child but my older one had a bit more of a phobia for needles and could still handle a shot in the mouth. She suggested that we should to nitrous/ laughing gas but I really wasn't comfortable with that. She again insisted and that it just made the whole experience less traumatic for the child. When we came back and I again expressed my concern about nitrous she again insisted that it was not a big deal, but in fact it was extremely traumatic.. not for him but for me. This is a great small little Japanese eatery. They replaced a sushi place we used to visit frequently and it to my wife and I too long to try it this place, but once we had dinner there, we went back the very next day for lunch; they're that good.

<review>We ordered a Tuna Sushi Burrito, Spicy Miso Ramen and Takoyaki.

Staff was very attentive and quick.

Tuna Sushi Burrito: Flavors and texture were on point. The rice was a thin layer but not too thin where it broke. The garlic chips and 2 sauces as a dip was a plus. We ordered a Super size and shared, still very large portion.

Spicy Miso Ramen: It was not very spicy, broth was good but nothing unique. The noodles were way too much, so much we barely got any broth. The noodles were also weird, not the right noodles used for Japanese ramen. They used Chinese egg noodles. They also give you only half a soft flavored egg. What a tease!

Takoyaki: Yummy! They had the right sauces and I love the Bonito flakes!</review><user>107135160095019803258< /user>< Pictures>

<Review>Based on all the reviews I was excited to try this place out. Interesting menu choices from sushi, ramen, udon, salads, and burgers. We got the ramen, fried chicken, the free gyoza (via yelp checkin), and a caterpillar roll. The best thing was the roll. The ramen was ok, but seemed to be lacking something. The broth felt overly fatty. Fried chicken was also ok. And the gyoza was ugh.

Right in the middle of our meal all the lights turned off. I thought we had a blackout for a moment when all of a sudden one of the waiters starts shaking a tambourine. Then party lights started flashing and the wait staff sang happy birthday to one of the customers. Once it was over all the lights came back on. Never seen such a show at any ramen place before.

The building looks like it was an old Taco Bell. Complete with drive-through. The parking is ok but you have to watch out for the drive-through cars. No wifi is offered here. From the outside the place seems a bit shady.

The staff was friendly, helpful, and attentive.<//Review>< pictures>

<resp>None</resp><Text>The GF and I have been faithful Kaiba customers for many years now, I'm surprised I haven't written a review before this point. <user>113326549642047333799</user><Name>Pedro Marquez</Name><time>1565236323016<//time><rate>5</rate>< text>
This is one of my favorite places to eat! A lot of people discount it because it has a drive through but that shouldn't stop you. The custom service here is excellent, your food order comes quickly, and it is always delicious. My go to items are the dragon roll and the tokantsu ramen. This place used to be a burger restaurant. Kaiba came in and used the Drive thru to its advantage. Even through the drive thur you get great service and great food. The o ly thing is just because you're going through drive thru don't expect fast food speed. It takes a bit longer than an average drive thru does but it's definitely worth the wait.</text>

< Review>
This is my go-to sushi restaurant. I stick with three items, although there are plenty other options. My top three choices are 1) Jalapeno bomb, 2) Salmon Burrito (warning, the large stands up to its name, and if you want to eat something else, do yourself a favor and order a mini), and 3) Crunch Asparagus. I often pair my meal with their $2 draft Sapporo that is so cold there are ice chips floating at the top. Be sure to do a Yelp check-in for a free starter, drink (non acholic), or ice cream. The staff is friendly, and most often attentive, but they're working on hiring more people, so this should soon be remedied. Last fun fact, they have a drive thru. Yep, a sushi joint where you don't even need to leave your car to order.<//Review>
